					<script>
						var $ = jQuery.noConflict();

						$(window).load(function () {
							var precios;
							var tallas;
							var colores;
							var url;

							// this is for the sort by select
							$(document).on("change","select",function(){
								$("option[value=" + this.value + "]", this)
								.attr("selected", true).siblings()
								.removeAttr("selected")

								url = url + "&orderby=" + $("select.orderby").children("option:selected").val();

								$("#filtrar_button").attr("href", url);

							});
							
							// this is for all other fields
							$(".filters_scroll input").change( function() {

								// empty arrays
								precios = "";
								tallas = "";
								colores = "";
							
								// check for precios
								$(".filters_scroll .options_precio input:checkbox:checked").each(function(){
									if (precios === "") {
										precios = $(this).val();
									}
									else {
										precios = precios + "," + $(this).val();
									}
								});

								// check for talals
								$(".filters_scroll .options_talla input:checkbox:checked").each(function(){
									if (tallas === "") {
										tallas = $(this).val();
									}
									else {
										tallas = tallas + "," + $(this).val();
									}
								});

								// check for colores
								$(".filters_scroll .options_color input:checkbox:checked").each(function(){
									if (colores === "") {
										colores = $(this).val();
									}
									else {
										colores = colores + "," + $(this).val();
									}
								});

								// alert("Precio : "+precios);
								// alert("Talla : "+tallas);
								// alert("Color : "+colores);

								url = document.location.protocol +"//"+ document.location.hostname + document.location.pathname + "?" ;

								if(precios) {
									var splitPrecios = precios.split(',');
									if(splitPrecios.length > 0) {

										var minPrecioRango = splitPrecios[0];
										var splitMinPrecioRango = minPrecioRango.split('_');
										var minPrecio = "&min_price=" + splitMinPrecioRango[0];

										var maxPrecioRango = splitPrecios[(splitPrecios.length)-1];
										var splitMaxPrecioRango = maxPrecioRango.split('_');
										var maxPrecio = "&max_price=" + splitMaxPrecioRango[1];

										url = url + minPrecio + maxPrecio;

									}
								}
								if(tallas) {
									url = url + "&filter_talla=" + tallas + "&query_type_talla=or";
								}
								if(colores) {
									url = url + "&filter_color=" + colores + "&query_type_color=or";
								}

								//url = document.location.protocol +"//"+ document.location.hostname + document.location.pathname + "?" + if(minPrecio){minPrecio} + if(maxPrecio){maxPrecio} + tallas_url + colores_url;

								$("#filtrar_button").attr("href", url);

								//alert(url);

							});
						});
					</script>

				</div>
			</div>
			</div>
</div>
